------------------------------------------------
-- DDL Statements for Table "RCTG01995_HUB_STAGE"."MV_PURGE_CAND_LIST"
------------------------------------------------
 SET CURRENT SCHEMA = "ISHWMTP3";
SET CURRENT PATH = "SYSIBM","SYSFUN","SYSPROC","SYSIBMADM","ISHWMTP3";

Create summary table RCTG01995_HUB_STAGE.MV_PURGE_CAND_LIST (CAND_NO) as (SELECT   CAND_NO FROM     (Select CAND_NO, sum(CAND_EXT) as CANDEXT, sum(CAND_OLD) AS CANDOLD, sum(EU_REQ_OLD) AS EUREQOLD, sum(NON_EU_REQ_OLD) AS NONEUREQOLD from (Select C.CAND_NO, case C.INT_CAND when 'No' then 'External' else 'Internal' end AS InternalExternal, case when C.INT_CAND = 'No' then 0 else 1 end AS CAND_EXT, C.INC_LAST_MOD_DT, C.INC_LAST_MOD_DT + 1 year AS CAND_OLD_DATE, case when C.INC_LAST_MOD_DT + 1 year < current_date then 0 else 1 end AS CAND_OLD, A.REQ_NO, R.LASTMODIFIEDDATE, R.LASTMODIFIEDDATE + 1 year AS REQONEYEAR, R.LASTMODIFIEDDATE + 5 year AS REQFIVEYEAR, NWLOC1.NAME AS COUNTRY, NWLOC1.NUMBER, case when NWLOC1.NUMBER in (1010,1056,1078,1057,1098,1102,1138,1159,1172,1180,1220,1077,1132) then case when R.LASTMODIFIEDDATE + 1 year < current_date then 0 else 1 end else 0 end AS EU_REQ_OLD, case when NWLOC1.NUMBER not in (1010,1056,1078,1057,1098,1102,1138,1159,1172,1180,1220,1077,1132) then case when R.LASTMODIFIEDDATE + 5 year < current_date then 0 else 1 end else 0 end AS NON_EU_REQ_OLD from RCTG01995_HUB_STAGE.CANDIDATE C left outer join RCTG01995_HUB_STAGE.APPLICATION A on C.CAND_NO = A.CAND_NO left outer join RCTG01995_HUB_STAGE.REQUISITION R on A.REQ_NO = R.REQ_NO left outer join RCTG01995_HUB_STAGE.LOCATION LOC on R.PRIMARYLOCATIONNO = LOC.NUMBER left outer join RCTG01995_HUB_STAGE.NETWORKLOCATION NWLOC4 on LOC.NW_LOC_NO = NWLOC4.NUMBER and NWLOC4.LEVEL = 4 left outer join RCTG01995_HUB_STAGE.NETWORKLOCATION NWLOC3 on LOC.NW_LOC_NO = NWLOC3.NUMBER and NWLOC3.LEVEL = 3 or NWLOC3.NUMBER = NWLOC4.PARENT_NO left outer join RCTG01995_HUB_STAGE.NETWORKLOCATION NWLOC2 on LOC.NW_LOC_NO = NWLOC2.NUMBER and NWLOC2.LEVEL = 2 or NWLOC2.NUMBER = NWLOC3.PARENT_NO left outer join RCTG01995_HUB_STAGE.NETWORKLOCATION NWLOC1 on LOC.NW_LOC_NO = NWLOC1.NUMBER and NWLOC1.LEVEL = 1 or NWLOC1.NUMBER = NWLOC2.PARENT_NO ) group by CAND_NO) WHERE    CANDEXT = 0 AND      CANDOLD = 0 AND      EUREQOLD = 0 AND      NONEUREQOLD = 0) DATA INITIALLY DEFERRED REFRESH DEFERRED ENABLE QUERY OPTIMIZATION MAINTAINED BY SYSTEM COMPRESS YES ADAPTIVE 		IN "P01995W5D032K" INDEX IN "P01995W5I032K" 		ORGANIZE BY ROW;

-- DDL Statements for User Defined Functions

SET SYSIBM.NLS_STRING_UNITS = 'SYSTEM';
SET CURRENT SCHEMA = "ISHWMTP3";
SET CURRENT PATH = "SYSIBM","SYSFUN","SYSPROC","SYSIBMADM","ISHWMTP3";

CREATE FUNCTION EXPLAIN_GET_MSGS( EXPLAIN_REQUESTER VARCHAR(128),
                                  EXPLAIN_TIME      TIMESTAMP,
                                  SOURCE_NAME       VARCHAR(128),
                                  SOURCE_SCHEMA     VARCHAR(128),
                                  SOURCE_VERSION    VARCHAR(64),
                                  EXPLAIN_LEVEL     CHAR(1),
                                  STMTNO            INTEGER,
                                  SECTNO            INTEGER,
                                  INLOCALE          VARCHAR(33) )
  RETURNS TABLE ( EXPLAIN_REQUESTER VARCHAR(128),
                  EXPLAIN_TIME      TIMESTAMP,
                  SOURCE_NAME       VARCHAR(128),
                  SOURCE_SCHEMA     VARCHAR(128),
                  SOURCE_VERSION    VARCHAR(64),
                  EXPLAIN_LEVEL     CHAR(1),
                  STMTNO            INTEGER,
                  SECTNO            INTEGER,
                  DIAGNOSTIC_ID     INTEGER,
                  LOCALE            VARCHAR(33),
                  MSG               VARCHAR(4096) )
  SPECIFIC EXPLAIN_GET_MSGS
  LANGUAGE SQL
  DETERMINISTIC
  NO EXTERNAL ACTION
  READS SQL DATA
  RETURN SELECT A.A_EXPLAIN_REQUESTER,
                A.A_EXPLAIN_TIME,
                A.A_SOURCE_NAME,
                A.A_SOURCE_SCHEMA,
                A.A_SOURCE_VERSION,
                A.A_EXPLAIN_LEVEL,
                A.A_STMTNO,
                A.A_SECTNO,
                A.A_DIAGNOSTIC_ID,
                F.LOCALE,
                F.MSG
         FROM EXPLAIN_DIAGNOSTIC A( A_EXPLAIN_REQUESTER,
                                    A_EXPLAIN_TIME,
                                    A_SOURCE_NAME,
                                    A_SOURCE_SCHEMA,
                                    A_SOURCE_VERSION,
                                    A_EXPLAIN_LEVEL,
                                    A_STMTNO,
                                    A_SECTNO,
                                    A_DIAGNOSTIC_ID,
                                    A_CODE ),
              TABLE( SYSPROC.EXPLAIN_GET_MSG2(
                       INLOCALE,
                       A.A_CODE,
                       ( SELECT TOKEN FROM EXPLAIN_DIAGNOSTIC_DATA B
                         WHERE A.A_EXPLAIN_REQUESTER = B.EXPLAIN_REQUESTER
                           AND A.A_EXPLAIN_TIME      = B.EXPLAIN_TIME
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_NAME       = B.SOURCE_NAME
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_SCHEMA     = B.SOURCE_SCHEMA
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_VERSION    = B.SOURCE_VERSION
                           AND A.A_EXPLAIN_LEVEL     = B.EXPLAIN_LEVEL
                           AND A.A_STMTNO            = B.STMTNO
                           AND A.A_SECTNO            = B.SECTNO
                           AND A.A_DIAGNOSTIC_ID     = B.DIAGNOSTIC_ID
                           AND B.ORDINAL=1 ),
                       ( SELECT TOKEN FROM EXPLAIN_DIAGNOSTIC_DATA B
                         WHERE A.A_EXPLAIN_REQUESTER = B.EXPLAIN_REQUESTER
                           AND A.A_EXPLAIN_TIME      = B.EXPLAIN_TIME
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_NAME       = B.SOURCE_NAME
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_SCHEMA     = B.SOURCE_SCHEMA

                           AND A.A_SOURCE_VERSION    = B.SOURCE_VERSION
                           AND A.A_EXPLAIN_LEVEL     = B.EXPLAIN_LEVEL
                           AND A.A_STMTNO            = B.STMTNO
                           AND A.A_SECTNO            = B.SECTNO
                           AND A.A_DIAGNOSTIC_ID     = B.DIAGNOSTIC_ID
                           AND B.ORDINAL=2 ),
                       ( SELECT TOKEN FROM EXPLAIN_DIAGNOSTIC_DATA B
                         WHERE A.A_EXPLAIN_REQUESTER = B.EXPLAIN_REQUESTER
                           AND A.A_EXPLAIN_TIME      = B.EXPLAIN_TIME
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_NAME       = B.SOURCE_NAME
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_SCHEMA     = B.SOURCE_SCHEMA
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_VERSION    = B.SOURCE_VERSION
                           AND A.A_EXPLAIN_LEVEL     = B.EXPLAIN_LEVEL
                           AND A.A_STMTNO            = B.STMTNO
                           AND A.A_SECTNO            = B.SECTNO
                           AND A.A_DIAGNOSTIC_ID     = B.DIAGNOSTIC_ID
                           AND B.ORDINAL=3 ) ) ) F
         WHERE ( EXPLAIN_REQUESTER IS NULL OR
                 EXPLAIN_REQUESTER = A.A_EXPLAIN_REQUESTER )
           AND ( EXPLAIN_TIME      IS NULL OR
                 EXPLAIN_TIME      = A.A_EXPLAIN_TIME      )
           AND ( SOURCE_NAME       IS NULL OR
                 SOURCE_NAME       = A.A_SOURCE_NAME       )
           AND ( SOURCE_SCHEMA     IS NULL OR
                 SOURCE_SCHEMA     = A.A_SOURCE_SCHEMA     )
           AND ( SOURCE_VERSION    IS NULL OR
                 SOURCE_VERSION    = A.A_SOURCE_VERSION    )
           AND ( EXPLAIN_LEVEL     IS NULL OR
                 EXPLAIN_LEVEL     = A.A_EXPLAIN_LEVEL     )
           AND ( STMTNO            IS NULL OR
                 STMTNO            = A.A_STMTNO            )
           AND ( SECTNO            IS NULL OR
                 SECTNO            = A.A_SECTNO            );


SET SYSIBM.NLS_STRING_UNITS = 'SYSTEM';
SET CURRENT SCHEMA = "T01995RP";

CREATE FUNCTION EXPLAIN_GET_MSGS( EXPLAIN_REQUESTER VARCHAR(128 OCTETS),
                                  EXPLAIN_TIME      TIMESTAMP,
                                  SOURCE_NAME       VARCHAR(128 OCTETS),
                                  SOURCE_SCHEMA     VARCHAR(128 OCTETS),
                                  SOURCE_VERSION    VARCHAR(64 OCTETS),
                                  EXPLAIN_LEVEL     CHAR(1 OCTETS),
                                  STMTNO            INTEGER,
                                  SECTNO            INTEGER,
                                  INLOCALE          VARCHAR(33 OCTETS) )
  RETURNS TABLE ( EXPLAIN_REQUESTER VARCHAR(128 OCTETS),
                  EXPLAIN_TIME      TIMESTAMP,
                  SOURCE_NAME       VARCHAR(128 OCTETS),
                  SOURCE_SCHEMA     VARCHAR(128 OCTETS),
                  SOURCE_VERSION    VARCHAR(64 OCTETS),
                  EXPLAIN_LEVEL     CHAR(1 OCTETS),
                  STMTNO            INTEGER,
                  SECTNO            INTEGER,
                  DIAGNOSTIC_ID     INTEGER,
                  LOCALE            VARCHAR(33 OCTETS),
                  MSG               VARCHAR(4096 OCTETS) )
  SPECIFIC EXPLAIN_GET_MSGS
  LANGUAGE SQL
  DETERMINISTIC
  NO EXTERNAL ACTION
  READS SQL DATA
  RETURN SELECT A.A_EXPLAIN_REQUESTER,
                A.A_EXPLAIN_TIME,
                A.A_SOURCE_NAME,
                A.A_SOURCE_SCHEMA,
                A.A_SOURCE_VERSION,
                A.A_EXPLAIN_LEVEL,
                A.A_STMTNO,
                A.A_SECTNO,
                A.A_DIAGNOSTIC_ID,
                F.LOCALE,
                F.MSG
         FROM EXPLAIN_DIAGNOSTIC A( A_EXPLAIN_REQUESTER,
                                    A_EXPLAIN_TIME,
                                    A_SOURCE_NAME,
                                    A_SOURCE_SCHEMA,
                                    A_SOURCE_VERSION,
                                    A_EXPLAIN_LEVEL,
                                    A_STMTNO,
                                    A_SECTNO,
                                    A_DIAGNOSTIC_ID,
                                    A_CODE ),
              TABLE( SYSPROC.EXPLAIN_GET_MSG2(
                       INLOCALE,
                       A.A_CODE,
                       ( SELECT TOKEN FROM EXPLAIN_DIAGNOSTIC_DATA B
                         WHERE A.A_EXPLAIN_REQUESTER = B.EXPLAIN_REQUESTER
                           AND A.A_EXPLAIN_TIME      = B.EXPLAIN_TIME
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_NAME       = B.SOURCE_NAME
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_SCHEMA     = B.SOURCE_SCHEMA
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_VERSION    = B.SOURCE_VERSION
                           AND A.A_EXPLAIN_LEVEL     = B.EXPLAIN_LEVEL
                           AND A.A_STMTNO            = B.STMTNO
                           AND A.A_SECTNO            = B.SECTNO
                           AND A.A_DIAGNOSTIC_ID     = B.DIAGNOSTIC_ID
                           AND B.ORDINAL=1 ),
                       ( SELECT TOKEN FROM EXPLAIN_DIAGNOSTIC_DATA B
                         WHERE A.A_EXPLAIN_REQUESTER = B.EXPLAIN_REQUESTER
                           AND A.A_EXPLAIN_TIME      = B.EXPLAIN_TIME
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_NAME       = B.SOURCE_NAME
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_SCHEMA     = B.SOURCE_SCHEMA

                           AND A.A_SOURCE_VERSION    = B.SOURCE_VERSION
                           AND A.A_EXPLAIN_LEVEL     = B.EXPLAIN_LEVEL
                           AND A.A_STMTNO            = B.STMTNO
                           AND A.A_SECTNO            = B.SECTNO
                           AND A.A_DIAGNOSTIC_ID     = B.DIAGNOSTIC_ID
                           AND B.ORDINAL=2 ),
                       ( SELECT TOKEN FROM EXPLAIN_DIAGNOSTIC_DATA B
                         WHERE A.A_EXPLAIN_REQUESTER = B.EXPLAIN_REQUESTER
                           AND A.A_EXPLAIN_TIME      = B.EXPLAIN_TIME
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_NAME       = B.SOURCE_NAME
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_SCHEMA     = B.SOURCE_SCHEMA
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_VERSION    = B.SOURCE_VERSION
                           AND A.A_EXPLAIN_LEVEL     = B.EXPLAIN_LEVEL
                           AND A.A_STMTNO            = B.STMTNO
                           AND A.A_SECTNO            = B.SECTNO
                           AND A.A_DIAGNOSTIC_ID     = B.DIAGNOSTIC_ID
                           AND B.ORDINAL=3 ) ) ) F
         WHERE ( EXPLAIN_REQUESTER IS NULL OR
                 EXPLAIN_REQUESTER = A.A_EXPLAIN_REQUESTER )
           AND ( EXPLAIN_TIME      IS NULL OR
                 EXPLAIN_TIME      = A.A_EXPLAIN_TIME      )

                 SOURCE_VERSION    = A.A_SOURCE_VERSION    )
           AND ( EXPLAIN_LEVEL     IS NULL OR
                 EXPLAIN_LEVEL     = A.A_EXPLAIN_LEVEL     )
           AND ( STMTNO            IS NULL OR
                 STMTNO            = A.A_STMTNO            )
           AND ( SECTNO            IS NULL OR
                 SECTNO            = A.A_SECTNO            );

                                  EXPLAIN_TIME      TIMESTAMP,
                                  SOURCE_NAME       VARCHAR(128 OCTETS),
                                  SOURCE_SCHEMA     VARCHAR(128 OCTETS),
                                  SOURCE_VERSION    VARCHAR(64 OCTETS),
                                  EXPLAIN_LEVEL     CHAR(1 OCTETS),
                                  STMTNO            INTEGER,
                                  SECTNO            INTEGER,
                                  INLOCALE          VARCHAR(33 OCTETS) )
  RETURNS TABLE ( EXPLAIN_REQUESTER VARCHAR(128 OCTETS),
                  EXPLAIN_TIME      TIMESTAMP,
                  SOURCE_NAME       VARCHAR(128 OCTETS),
                  SOURCE_SCHEMA     VARCHAR(128 OCTETS),
                  SOURCE_VERSION    VARCHAR(64 OCTETS),
                  EXPLAIN_LEVEL     CHAR(1 OCTETS),
                  STMTNO            INTEGER,
                  SECTNO            INTEGER,
                  DIAGNOSTIC_ID     INTEGER,
                  LOCALE            VARCHAR(33 OCTETS),
                  MSG               VARCHAR(4096 OCTETS) )
  SPECIFIC EXPLAIN_GET_MSGS
  LANGUAGE SQL
  DETERMINISTIC
  NO EXTERNAL ACTION
  READS SQL DATA
  RETURN SELECT A.A_EXPLAIN_REQUESTER,
                A.A_EXPLAIN_TIME,
                A.A_SOURCE_NAME,
                A.A_SOURCE_SCHEMA,
                A.A_SOURCE_VERSION,
                A.A_EXPLAIN_LEVEL,
                A.A_STMTNO,
                A.A_SECTNO,
                A.A_DIAGNOSTIC_ID,
                F.LOCALE,
                F.MSG
         FROM EXPLAIN_DIAGNOSTIC A( A_EXPLAIN_REQUESTER,
                                    A_EXPLAIN_TIME,
                                    A_SOURCE_NAME,
                                    A_SOURCE_SCHEMA,
                                    A_SOURCE_VERSION,
                                    A_EXPLAIN_LEVEL,
                                    A_STMTNO,
                                    A_SECTNO,
                                    A_DIAGNOSTIC_ID,
                                    A_CODE ),
              TABLE( SYSPROC.EXPLAIN_GET_MSG2(
                       INLOCALE,
                       A.A_CODE,
                       ( SELECT TOKEN FROM EXPLAIN_DIAGNOSTIC_DATA B
                         WHERE A.A_EXPLAIN_REQUESTER = B.EXPLAIN_REQUESTER
                           AND A.A_EXPLAIN_TIME      = B.EXPLAIN_TIME
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_NAME       = B.SOURCE_NAME
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_SCHEMA     = B.SOURCE_SCHEMA
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_VERSION    = B.SOURCE_VERSION
                           AND A.A_EXPLAIN_LEVEL     = B.EXPLAIN_LEVEL
                           AND A.A_STMTNO            = B.STMTNO
                           AND A.A_SECTNO            = B.SECTNO
                           AND A.A_DIAGNOSTIC_ID     = B.DIAGNOSTIC_ID
                           AND B.ORDINAL=1 ),
                       ( SELECT TOKEN FROM EXPLAIN_DIAGNOSTIC_DATA B
                         WHERE A.A_EXPLAIN_REQUESTER = B.EXPLAIN_REQUESTER
                           AND A.A_EXPLAIN_TIME      = B.EXPLAIN_TIME
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_NAME       = B.SOURCE_NAME
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_SCHEMA     = B.SOURCE_SCHEMA

                           AND A.A_SOURCE_VERSION    = B.SOURCE_VERSION
                           AND A.A_EXPLAIN_LEVEL     = B.EXPLAIN_LEVEL
                           AND A.A_STMTNO            = B.STMTNO
                           AND A.A_SECTNO            = B.SECTNO
                           AND A.A_DIAGNOSTIC_ID     = B.DIAGNOSTIC_ID
                           AND B.ORDINAL=2 ),
                       ( SELECT TOKEN FROM EXPLAIN_DIAGNOSTIC_DATA B
                         WHERE A.A_EXPLAIN_REQUESTER = B.EXPLAIN_REQUESTER
                           AND A.A_EXPLAIN_TIME      = B.EXPLAIN_TIME
                           AND A.A_SOURCE_NAME       = B.SOURCE_NAME

                           AND A.A_SECTNO            = B.SECTNO
                           AND A.A_DIAGNOSTIC_ID     = B.DIAGNOSTIC_ID
                           AND B.ORDINAL=3 ) ) ) F
         WHERE ( EXPLAIN_REQUESTER IS NULL OR
                 EXPLAIN_REQUESTER = A.A_EXPLAIN_REQUESTER )
